# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="381a4-102">Tipos obsoletos en .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="381a4-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="381a4-103"><a name="introduction"></a> En las tablas de este artículo se muestran los tipos que están obsoletos en [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] y [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)] organizados por ensamblados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="381a4-103"><a name="introduction"></a> The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="381a4-104">Utilice los vínculos siguientes para ver una lista de tipos obsoletos y las alternativas recomendadas en cada ensamblado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="381a4-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="381a4-105">Dado que estos tipos están en desuso, todos sus miembros también lo están.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="381a4-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="381a4-106">Para obtener una lista de miembros obsoletos adicionales de la biblioteca de clases de .NET Framework, vea [Miembros obsoletos](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="381a4-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

## <a name="obsolete-types-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="381a4-133">Tipos obsoletos en ensamblados del sistema</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="381a4-133">Obsolete Types in System Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="381a4-134">En las tablas siguientes se enumeran los tipos que se han declarado obsoletos en ensamblados del sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="381a4-134">The following tables list the types that have been declared obsolete in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="381a4-135">Estos ensamblados se usan para el desarrollo de aplicaciones de uso\-general cuyo destino es .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="381a4-135">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>

## <a name="obsolete-types-in-microsoft-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="381a4-925">Tipos obsoletos en ensamblados de Microsoft</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="381a4-925">Obsolete Types in Microsoft Assemblies</span></span>
